Yesterday's News on the Labor Strike at the Shishi Xinbao 61

Widespread Condolences The Newspaper Industry Union issued a message stating that the Shanghai Shishi Xinbao authorities had, on this occasion, groundlessly expelled workers, blockaded the workplace, and illegally detained workers, causing labor-management disputes. Although powerful figures had been appointed to mediate, the management showed no sincerity, almost causing a breakdown. Details had already been reported in the newspapers. Various groups in Shanghai, fearing that both parties would take extreme measures, continued to make great efforts to mediate and sent personnel to express their condolences to the workers of the newspaper. The situation yesterday is summarized below.

Postal Workers Mediate The Shanghai Postal Workers Union, upon hearing that mediation between the two sides had failed, sent representatives Yu Songqiao and Cheng Zuoqing to express their condolences yesterday afternoon at 3 PM. They expressed their indignation at the improper actions taken by the newspaper management on this occasion and were reportedly preparing to send representatives to mediate with the management. If the management again showed no sincerity in resolving the matter, they would resolutely provide support with their strength.

Union's Attitude The person in charge of the Newspaper Industry Union told reporters that the means of destruction employed by the capitalists were endless. For example, the advertisement recently published to register all workers, after careful study by the union, proves several points. 1. Why register old workers? 2. Various regulations and labor-management contracts have been signed, so why fill out a letter of willingness? 3. The cause of this incident was only the issue of printing the Da Wanbao newspaper, which had nothing to do with the newspaper itself. 4. No new demands were made in advance, and there were no illegal actions, so there was no such thing as willful arbitrariness and peace of mind. All of this proves that the capitalists deliberately destroyed the workers' organization, so the union is determined to do its best to deal with it.

Sending Condolences 1. Publishing Industry Industrial Union Organizing Committee (omitted above) All workers of the Shishi Xinbao under your association have recently been brutally destroyed by the management, relying on external forces. The news has caused deep indignation. The history of labor movement in your newspaper is glorious. This time, the leadership has oppressed the workers and engaged in struggle. The success of the great achievements can be predicted. Our association respectfully sends a brief letter and sends representatives Ge Hecai, Feng Jifang, etc. to express their condolences. We hope to make greater efforts to win the final victory. (omitted below) 2. First District Water and Electricity Industry Union, omitted above. On this occasion, the Shishi Xinbao management forced the workers of the museum to print the Da Wanbao newspaper, using various threatening means to destroy the labor movement, and using the amulet of imperialists to detain loyal workers, and even insult the members of your association, which is contrary to reason and illegal, which is extremely infuriating. In addition to being willing to be the backing of your association, we will send another special letter of condolence. (omitted below) 3. China Journalism Research Association. This time, your association was brutally suppressed by the capitalists, blockaded the workplace, and expelled workers because it refused to print the Da Wanbao, a trust newspaper industry. When our colleagues heard the news, they were all filled with righteous indignation. They unanimously decided to send comrades Chen Weizhong and Ye Qing to represent our association to express their condolences and hope that your association will fight with the capitalists and persist to the end. Our association will naturally be the backing of your association. (omitted below)

Letter to the Lawyers Association In addition, because the newspaper's employee Jiang Jiemin used a self-defense pistol to illegally arrest workers, violating the police law, the union sent a letter to the Lawyers Association, requesting the association to impose appropriate sanctions. The original letter is as follows: Sir, Jiang Jiemin, a member of your association, used a self-defense pistol at the intersection of Damalu Jiangxi Road at 2 AM on the 5th of this month to illegally arrest Ma Deren, Wu Miaosheng, Hu Wan, Shen Gengsheng, Zhang Wenquan, Chen Shixiang, Zhu Zuxing, and Wang Kegang, eight workers from our association. This is extremely wrong. Your association has always been committed to upholding justice and protecting human rights. Jiang Jiemin's illegal actions should be immediately expelled from membership as a warning to others and to protect the reputation of your association.

Yangtze River Waterway Entrance to Moor an Unattended Lightship 65

Haimu Section Circular No. 1026 of the General Taxation Department of the Customs General Administration: For the purpose of the circular, the General Tax Secretary ordered that an unattended lightship will be moored at the entrance of the Yangtze River Waterway under the jurisdiction of the Jianghai Customs to facilitate navigation. All matters concerning the installation of the ship shall be listed separately and ordered to be complied with by the tour worker. Hereby announce it, and copy all the items opened in the order, so that all Chinese and foreign shipping merchants know about it, and hereby announce it. The list is as follows: 1. Name of the lightship: Yangtze River Waterway Entrance Lightship, written on it: Yangtze Entrance 2. Anchorage: Entrance of the Yangtze River Waterway, view the Daji Mountain Light, Tower as due north 202 degrees, its distance is 9 nautical miles and 62 percent. 3. Lighting date: around May 12 this year, no more announcement will be made at that time. 4. Lightship situation: the hull is red, and Yangtze Entrance is written in foreign languages on both sides. A steel cylinder is erected on the deck, with a light placed on it. The light is 30 feet above the water surface. In sunny weather, the light can illuminate 11 nautical miles. There is a fog bell at the stern of the ship, suspended from a steel frame. The bell is struck by a hammer, and the hammer's movement is caused by the seawater washing the lightship. 5. Type of light: fourth-order lens flashing boat, bright for three seconds, dark for seven seconds. 6. Related books: Channel Chart No. 1011 of the Naval Department of the Republic of China. 7. Navigator's attention: Since the certificate ship is unattended, the anchor light is not lit. April 1, 21st year of the Republic of China, Haimu Section Tour Worker Xi Liman.

Details of the Preparatory Meeting 72

(Luoyang) The National Disaster Conference held a preparatory meeting at the National Disaster Conference venue in Xigong, Luoyang at 2 PM on the 7th. 148 members including Yan Guofu attended, 10 Central Committee members including Wang Faqin attended, Ru Yuli, Minister of the Audit Department of the National Government Supervisory Yuan, attended, Jin Zhi, representative of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government, and Chu Minyi, director of the secretariat, were present. A temporary report was made, proposing to invite Mr. Dai Ren, the oldest member, to be the temporary chairman of today's preparatory meeting to ask if there are any objections (the whole audience applauded and agreed) Temporary Chairman Dai Ren, Secretary Director Chu Minyi, Deputy Director Peng Xuepei, the chairman respectfully read the Prime Minister's will, 1. The Secretary Director reported the progress of this meeting, 2. To elect the presidium, the chairman inquired according to item 5 of the organizational outline of this meeting, "This meeting shall establish a presidium of three to five people, which shall be elected by the members." Now, please decide whether the number of the presidium should be three or five. Member Zhu Jingnong proposed to use the recorded vote method, with each ballot jointly electing five people, and the members voting freely. The chairman determined that the number of the presidium would be five, asking if there were any objections, there were no objections. The election of the five members of the presidium by free vote, asking if there were any objections, there were no objections. The chairman explained that each ballot for the election should jointly elect five people, and the electors must be registered. He also appointed four members, Gao Yihan, Zhu Jingnong, Li Zongtong, and Chang Hengfang, as ballot supervisors for the presidium election. The Secretary Director reported that a total of 159 ballots were issued, 148 members, 10 Central Committee members, and 1 government minister. The ballot supervisors counted the ballots on the spot. The Secretary Director reported the ballot count results, a total of 157 ballots, 2 abstentions. The Secretary Director reported the vote count results, 1. Wang Xiaolai received 66 votes, Zhang Boling received 40 votes, Gao Yihan received 37 votes, Liu Hengjing received 35 votes, and Tong Guanxian received 32 votes, and were elected as the presidium of this meeting, 2. The three people with the next highest number of votes, Zang Qifang 27 votes, Ma Yinchu 26 votes, Yang Ruifang 24 votes, 3. Sign the seating arrangement, 4. Resolution, to send a telegram to the members in Pingjin and Shanghai in the name of the members who attended today's preparatory meeting to come to the meeting immediately, and the telegram will be drafted by the secretariat and approved by the presidium, 5. Committee member Zhu Jingnong proposed a temporary motion that all important motions or reports regarding national defense, diplomacy and other matters must be approved by the presidium before they can be released to the public. Resolution approved and implemented. 6. President Wang proposed a temporary motion to invite Zhangjia Hutuktu, who will come to Luoyang in the future, to be the honorary chairman of this meeting to show respect. The resolution was passed. 7. Member Yu Senwen proposed a temporary motion to send a telegram in the name of this meeting to express condolences to the soldiers at the front. The resolution was passed and sent to the secretariat for drafting and approved by the presidium. (Seventh Daily Telegram)

Wang Jingwei's Opening Speech 73

(Luoyang) President Wang gave an opening speech at the opening ceremony of the National Disaster Conference on the 7th, saying that the holding of this National Disaster Conference was decided by the Fourth National Congress of the Chinese Kuomintang, and later decided by the First Plenary Session of the Fourth Central Committee. The National Disaster Conference should discuss matters related to resistance to aggression, disaster relief, and pacification. The National Government issued an order in January this year and decided to hold the meeting in Nanjing on February 1, but unfortunately, the Shanghai Incident occurred. The National Government moved to Luoyang on January 30, so the meeting could not be held as scheduled. Only today can the meeting be opened in Luoyang. This meeting is a manifestation of the consistent national consciousness of the Chinese nation. This national consciousness is the crystallization of more than 4,000 years of China, and is the only lifeline that supports the country for more than 4,000 years. Our national consciousness not only has national characteristics, but also has global characteristics. Internally, we seek the freedom and equality of ethnic groups within the country, and externally, we seek the freedom and equality of the entire Chinese nation in the world. Unfortunately, in our efforts to seek freedom and equality, Japan has continued to attack us. Conspiring to split my north and south in the Xin Hai year was the first step. The request for the 21 articles in the fourth year of the Republic of China was the second step. The Jinan Massacre in the seventeenth year was a plot to destroy my unification as the third step. Now it is making a fourth step attack, which is more serious than before. If we want to break through this difficult situation, we must promote national consciousness and strengthen unity and struggle. The most important task during the period of political tutelage is to awaken the masses, especially the productive masses. The so-called production includes spiritual production and material production. At present, the most important thing is that all spiritual and material producers work together. You are the most outstanding members of all producers. Now you are all in the National Disaster Conference, jointly seeking ways to solve the national crisis, and I believe that there will be great success in the future. In addition to paying tribute to you today, I have two more points to make. One is the issue of responsibility. The National Party Comrades fully bear the responsibility for the national crisis and cannot shirk it. We are very willing to accept everyone's assistance in holding this meeting today, but we never intend to shirk responsibility. The second is the issue of authority. The Executive Yuan prepared the National Disaster Conference in accordance with the order of the National Government, and the order of the National Government was based on the resolution of the Central Party. The National Disaster Conference discusses matters related to resistance to aggression, disaster relief, and pacification. Therefore, the Executive Yuan is of course responsible for answering questions within this scope. The Executive Yuan cannot answer questions outside this scope, but everyone can freely express their opinions. As for various issues related to military affairs, finance, diplomacy, and resistance to aggression, disaster relief, and pacification, the various departments of the Executive Yuan have already prepared to report to you. (Seventh Daily Telegram)

Speech by Member Tao Menghe 74

(Luoyang) At the opening ceremony of the National Crisis Conference, member representative Tao Menghe delivered a speech, roughly stating: 1. Regarding the location for holding this National Crisis Conference, some advocated for Nanjing, but after I arrived in the temporary capital, I felt that holding it in Luoyang was even better than Nanjing. This is because the recent history of the Republic of China has all taken place in areas with convenient transportation, and everyone lacks a deep understanding of the central interior. Now, being able to hold the National Crisis Conference in Luoyang will naturally allow for a deeper understanding of China's national conditions and the dangerous situation of the national crisis. 2. In the past one or two decades, we have not worked hard to carry out the national independence movement, quell internal strife, and ensure the solid and complete organization of the country. When the Kuomintang was in power, it could have earnestly implemented Mr. Sun Yat-sen's policies, but unfortunately, in reality, things did not go as desired, and our people did not unanimously urge the government to promote and expand national consciousness, making the country a very powerful entity that could stand in the turbulent Pacific situation. This responsibility should be borne jointly by all the people, but the Kuomintang should also bear considerable responsibility. Those participating in this meeting are willing to do their best to demonstrate that our national spirit and organization are extremely cohesive and powerful, and are even more willing to unanimously support the current government in implementing the resolutions of the conference to achieve the goal of resisting aggression. 3. If the people can strive to thoroughly implement Mr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings, then the Republic of China can undoubtedly become one of the most powerful countries along the Pacific coast. Before the Kuomintang's period of political tutelage is completed, how to begin to truly implement all of Mr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings is a fundamental question. As for whether the three major issues of resisting aggression, disaster relief, and pacification discussed in the conference can be implemented depends entirely on the power, policies, and methods of the current government authorities. We cannot but say that in the past few years, the realization of Sun Yat-sen's doctrine has not yet been achieved, but we still believe in the future of the Kuomintang. This belief is the hope that it can truly and thoroughly implement Mr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings in the future. We come to this meeting from this standpoint, and we hope that the chairman can convey the contributions of the members' discussions to the government, and even more hope that the government authorities can adopt or refer to them as much as possible. (7th Dispatch)

The International Investigation Team's Special Train Has Passed Yucheng 75

Visited various scenic spots when passing through Jinan, and inspected traces of Japanese artillery shells. (Jinan) The League of Nations investigation team's train, with an armored car marked "Beiping" leading the way, arrived at Jinan at 3:50 PM. They first arrived at the ancient Lixia Pavilion. The team expressed great respect upon seeing a portrait of Confucius. Then, they went to the library and greatly admired the Song and Yuan books and ancient zithers, saying that sculpture and music were both introduced to the West from China. Gu Weijun led the team to visit the traces of Japanese artillery shells from the May 3rd Incident. Lytton was quite surprised. Gu told reporters that the Northeast opposed his visit, but there was no formal statement. He would, of course, go. The Northeast's unwillingness for him to go was within expectations. Then, they boarded the boats again and went to the North Pole Pavilion, then changed to cars to tour the city's main roads, returning to the station at 7:05 PM. Lytton nodded and returned the greeting from inside the train until the train left the platform. On this day, Zhang Shaotang, the secretary-general of the provincial government, waited for the team at the provincial government on behalf of Han. Gu Weijun introduced them. Today, flags were hung throughout the city, and the streets were cleared. (8th Dispatch)

In short, it is hoped that the team will complete its peace mission with an impartial attitude and that the investigation will be successful, so that world peace and prosperity can be maintained. Passed Through Xuzhou Late at Night Without Being Welcomed 78

(Xuzhou) The League of Nations investigation team's special train left Pukou at 4:00 PM on the 7th and passed through Bengbu at 10:00 PM, arriving in Xuzhou at 3:30 AM on the 8th. A welcome slogan in Chinese, English, and French was made on the overpass of the Xuzhou station, and the electric lights shone extremely brightly. Representatives from all walks of life had already arrived at the station earlier to greet them and had prepared a welcome speech, pushing Feng Jieren to deliver the speech in English. Later, Qian Zongyuan, the director of the Jinpu Railway's on-train reception, sent a telegram from Bengbu, stating that he had received instructions from Representative Gu that the special train arrived in Xuzhou in the middle of the night, and all the representatives were already asleep, so he requested that all greetings be waived. Therefore, they temporarily dispersed. When the train arrived at the station, personnel from the Jinpu and Longhai Railways took care of it at the station, and the order was extremely quiet. At 4:30 AM, the train departed northward, scheduled to arrive in Jinan at 4:00 PM for an inspection of the traces of the May 3rd Massacre, and scheduled to arrive in Tianjin at 9:00 AM on the 9th. The train consisted of a total of eighteen cars, towed by locomotive number 287, which was replaced by locomotive number 279 in Xuzhou to tow it north. Between Pukou-Xuzhou and Xuzhou-Dezhou, the 3rd and 1st Railway Artillery Teams followed the train, with armored cars in the front and rear, providing extremely thorough security. (8th Dispatch)

(Xuzhou) Qian Zongyuan told reporters that the investigation team's representatives felt very comfortable on the train here, saying that it exceeded their ideal vehicle. The representatives held a meeting on the Longhe ship on the morning of the 7th before boarding the train to discuss Representative Gu's visit to the Northeast. The representatives believed that they were commissioned by the League of Nations to conduct an open investigation and treat both China and Japan with an equal spirit, without allowing any discrimination. Since the Japanese representatives had already participated, the Chinese representatives should also go. They unanimously agreed to Gu's visit to the Northeast. When passing through Chuzhou and Bengbu, representatives from all walks of life were granted an audience, and were received by the German representative. The Japanese representative Yoshida always accompanied him, so the representatives had little to say to the welcoming representatives, responding with a smile. As for his own mission, he was fully responsible for the reception on the Jinpu line, he said. (8th Dispatch)

(Xuzhou) When the League of Nations investigation team passed through Xuzhou, a certain foreigner spoke to reporters at the station in a private capacity, saying that Japan's refusal of Representative Gu to go to the Northeast was completely unreasonable. Gu was invited by the investigation team, and refusing Gu was tantamount to opposing the investigation team, and also tantamount to opposing the League of Nations. As for the refusal to allow the Chinese side's prepared train to pass through the border, it is even more unconscious. The same vehicle is travelling the same route, why not be responsible for its protection? Moreover, the Northeast is still Chinese territory, but it is temporarily occupied by the Japanese army. Looking at America's boycott of Japanese goods, the Japanese dare not say a word, showing that the means of coercion are applied selectively. Having lived in China for a long time, I sincerely hope that the Chinese people can strive to strengthen themselves and avenge this humiliation, he said. (8th Dispatch)

Seeing that the two Chinese investigators were both carrying handguns, and hearing the sound of "robbers" being shouted, they assumed that these two were the bandits and opened fire. Four-Power Conference on Danube River Problem Breaks Down 134

British and French Differ with German and Italian Views, Conference Reaches Stalemate. Germany Opposes Preferential Tax Rates. Bulgaria Demands Membership. Representatives Employ Political Maneuvering, Unable to Shake Off Centuries of Bad Habits.

Reuter, London, 7th: It is heard that the Four-Power Conference of England, France, Italy, and Germany will adjourn tomorrow and will probably reconvene in Geneva, as representatives from various countries will gather in Geneva next week to attend the disarmament conference. The committee studying the Danube River economic problems met all day, dispersing only at 5 PM. According to reliable sources, although the committee tried hard to find a solution to the problem, it ultimately failed to make real progress in reconciling the differences between England and France with Italy and Germany. England and France advocate the establishment of a union of Danube River countries, while Germany and Italy do not agree. The afternoon meeting was devoted to studying statistics and data on the economic conditions of the Danube River countries. However, the disagreement was the same as in the morning. Some parties expect that the four countries can eventually reach a consensus agreement, but some kind of data is being collected, which cannot be obtained in one or two hours, so an agreement may not be reached tomorrow. According to responsible sources, the main point discussed today was the suggestion that a certain country should abolish its rights under the most-favored-nation treaty with a certain country in the Danube River. It is heard that the committee agreed in principle that the Danube River countries must stand on a self-sufficient basis, and any assistance given by other countries should be based on enabling the countries to develop themselves without external assistance. Relying solely on external assistance is definitely not enough to avoid the collapse of the Danube River countries, and the Danube River countries should establish an agreement on their future happiness themselves. Italy and Germany believe that the conference will be ineffective unless all the Danube River countries participate, and they also argue that Italy and Bulgaria should be included in the Danube River countries. They also said that many other countries are also related to the trade of the Danube River countries, and their interests are also very complicated, so it is almost impossible to obtain proposals that suit all parties' interests. The conference proceeded with great sincerity on the surface, but the participants still used their manipulation skills, unable to shake off the old habits of European rival countries for centuries. This kind of political maneuvering made the economic difficulties suffered by the Danube River countries even more unmanageable, so the discussion resulted in a stalemate. Although the participants unanimously said that they should urgently find ways to save the Danube River countries from bankruptcy, the main problems were not mentioned after the meeting began. The main point of contention was whether the five Danube River countries should conclude a customs union, or whether each country should clearly stipulate treaties with third parties. They held different opinions and failed to agree, so the progress of the conference was suspended. According to the above two proposals, they must be approved by all countries in the world that have most-favored-nation treatment treaties with the Danube River countries. At a time when many European politicians are now suspecting each other of having treacherous intentions, Sir Arthur Salter, Director of the Financial and Economic Section of the League of Nations, has just published a book entitled "Recovery," which details the economic and political reasons that led to the current crisis. The knight contributed to European civilization in only two ways: one is to realize the ideal of common security, and the other is to mutually conclude military alliances and wage world wars. The knight also mentioned the significant losses caused by private financial groups arbitrarily providing loans. The loans granted by the Swedish Kreuger & Toll company to the Danube countries alone have approached 20 million English pounds.

Reuter, London, 8th: The Four-Power Conference broke down at 11:30 this morning because it could not agree on a plan to save the economic difficulties of the Danube River countries. According to the final communique, the major powers all believed that the Danube River countries and other countries should take joint action as a matter of urgency to place the Danube River countries on a solid foundation. This is also the first step in the recovery of the European economy. After the meeting was discussed, it was found that there were many economic points that needed to be further studied. Because the League of Nations will hold an important meeting next week, the Four-Power Conference cannot continue. However, the four countries will still exchange views on the reserved points and continue to make progress in the best way, etc. This proves that the bright hope that the Danube River countries could be saved early has now disappeared. The only hope left is that perhaps the exchange of views between diplomats and the economic discussions of the League of Nations can overcome all difficulties and achieve something. It is generally recognized that the British delegation made great efforts to reconcile the differences between all parties, but unfortunately, the conference still ended in failure due to divergent opinions. At the end of the meeting, Foreign Minister Grandi said, "The matter is over. We have done everything we can." The German chief representative, Bülow, said, "From the beginning, I knew that such a complex problem could not be solved in three days."

National News, London, 8th: The Four-Power Danube River Conference has resolutely rejected the proposal to organize a customs union in the Danube River basin, because it is equivalent to restoring the economic organization of the former Austro-Hungarian Empire. Not only are there many opponents, but also there are thorns everywhere, and it is very difficult to realize. Furthermore, in this conference, in fact, it was also unable to agree on how many countries should be included in the Danube River basin. In addition, the major powers are unwilling to abandon their most-favored-nation rights in their commercial agreements with the Danube River states, which is also a major reason why the conference has fallen into a stalemate, and it is an element that has contributed to the rejection of the proposal to organize a customs union, because the major powers, even for the temporary mutual levying of preferential tax rates among the Danube River states, do not wish to easily agree.

National News, Sofia, 8th: The Bulgarian government has instructed its ambassador to the United Kingdom to send a letter to the British government, reapplying for Bulgaria to be listed as one of the Danube River states in the economic agreement to rescue the Danube River proposed by the major powers. According to a press release, the Bulgarian official document strongly stated that the country's finances, like those of other Danube River states, are exhausted to the extreme. If it does not receive the same rescue, it will go bankrupt.

Ji Army, Ding and Li, Resolutely Resist Japan 137

Li Guilin's persuasion is ineffective. Anti-Japanese soldiers along the river recover Nong'an. Changchun, the puppet capital, is in great panic.

Harbin Communication: Xi Qia's enticement of Ding Chao and Li Du to surrender has recently been in vain. The issue in dispute is whether to hand over military power. Xi Qia only agreed to issue a batch of military pay, and refused all other requests. Ding and Li also refused to yield, so there were no results. Seeing that Ding and Li's resistance was very firm, the Japanese side forced Xi Qia's first and seventh brigades of the police and military on the 27th of last month to launch a sudden advance against the Liangzhuhe Self-Defense Army, intending to attack Ding and Li unprepared. However, the police brigades understood the Self-Defense Army and were unwilling to kill each other, so at the beginning of the battle, they only fired into the air. The Japanese army realized their intentions and immediately had the Amano Brigade supervise the battle from behind, using machine guns and artillery to suppress the front line. Therefore, the Self-Defense Army truly engaged the police brigades, and after a day of fighting, the Self-Defense Army was in a very advantageous position. However, Wang Zhiyou, who was negotiating peace in Harbin, was detained at this time. Xi Qia further telegraphed Li Guilin, using Wang's voice to persuade Ding and Li to cease fire. Li Guilin went to Liangzhuhe on a special train, still wanting to persuade Ding Chao in person. Ding, along with Zhao Yi, Feng Zhanhai, and others, avoided him and went to Yanshou. Only Xing Zhanqing and Chen Decai, because of their special relationship with Li, still met with Li. Li persuaded Xing and Chen to accept the conditions, gather at Yimianpo, and listen to the issuance of pay and reorganization. That night, Ding Chao received a letter in Yanshou and immediately ordered the Self-Defense Army to retreat to Fangzheng, to avoid military morale from collapsing. Xing and Chen's troops, with more than two thousand people, also retreated with Ding Chao, leaving less than four battalions who would listen to the reorganization. Li Guilin is still handling this matter on the Ha-Sui Line. After Ding Chao led his troops to retreat to Fangzheng, Yu Shenzheng led more than 10,000 of the puppet Jilin army, with the help of the Japanese army's Taniguchi and Ono brigades, launched a fierce attack on Fangzheng, fierce fighting for two days, several Japanese aircraft dropped bombs in the air, and fires broke out in many places in the city. The Self-Defense Army rescued the fire on one side and fought back on the other. The Japanese aircraft "Patriotic" flew very low while dropping bombs, and was shot down by the Self-Defense Army, and the driver died immediately. On the morning of the 31st, Gong Zhanhai's Self-Defense Army attacked and occupied Shixian County. At the same time, because the Japanese army rushed to Nong'an to reinforce, our army's strength was suddenly reduced, and the Self-Defense Army fiercely repelled Yu's army, and pursued them to the Gaolimaozi area, defeating a brigade of the puppet army. Fangzheng was then safe. Li Du is organizing military supplies and temporarily organizing volunteer armies in Yilan, for long-term resistance. The former National Salvation Army in Tailai Town, Heilongjiang Province, also arrived in Yilan, and was reorganized by Li into a detachment. Therefore, although there were fewer troops from Xing Zhanqing and Chen Decai, they were replaced by this, and the strength was not reduced. The Gong Zhanhai army, which occupied Binzhou, also retreated back to Fangzheng because Yu Shenzheng's troops cooperated with the Japanese army to counterattack. Yesterday, it was heard that there was still fierce fighting at Gaolimaozi, and Yu Shenzheng's puppet army was surrounded by the Self-Defense Army. The headquarters of the 2nd Division of the Japanese Army stationed in Harbin moved to Wujimi Station (140 li from Yimianpo) on the eastern section of the East China Railway on April 2. Personnel and supplies were transported by a special train. Division Commander Domon also followed, reportedly to launch a general attack on the national salvation armies of Wang Delin and Liu Zhenbang in Mudanjiang above Modaohezi. Wang Delin himself led his troops to attack along the Ji-Dun Railway. More than a thousand of Wang's troops have advanced to Mudanjiang Station on the eastern line. Liu Zhenbang's large army is in Muling, and recently recruited a large number of broadsword troops, numbering 2,000, with great momentum. The Japanese side is deeply worried, so it is anxious to attack, but it is also heard that the movement of the 2nd Division Headquarters is to facilitate the command of anti-Russian military affairs, and may need to be moved to Hengdaohezi in the future. As for the troops of the three brigades under Domon's command, except for the Murai Brigade being scattered along the Ha-Sui Line, the Amano and Taniguchi brigades rushed to Nong'an to reinforce on the 31st. The county seat of Nong'an is only 120 li away from Changchun, the puppet capital. At 5:00 AM on March 29, it was recovered by the 7,000 troops of Li Qingshan's National Salvation Volunteer Army, which had captured Fuyu. Liu Yukun's 1,500 troops of the first cavalry brigade stationed in the city had expelled their brigade commander and joined the National Salvation Army, so the recovery of the county seat was quite easy. The original Changchun Japanese Consulate Branch, consular staff and Japanese canvassers, and Japanese expatriates all fled to Changchun, causing great panic in the Changchun puppet court. Because there were not many stationed troops, 500 Japanese troops, 300 police, and Jin Bitong's 1,000-man garrison force took many cars to defend. On the way to Huangtulingzi (20 li from Nong'an), they were ambushed by the National Salvation Army, killing countless people and seizing seven carloads of supplies and ammunition. Only one car escaped. On the 30th, the Japanese side increased the Manchurian Railway garrison by 1,000 troops, together with Xi Qia's Ji-Chang garrison and seven Japanese aircraft to attack. The Japanese army launched a fierce artillery attack, and the city streets were destroyed by artillery fire, with countless military and civilian casualties. The volunteer army still calmly fought back. By the evening, the Japanese army was repelled. At noon on the 31st, the Japanese side changed to seven aircraft dropping bombs and bombing, and the merchants' residences in the city were destroyed by fire.

Investigation Team Travels from Hankou Through Nanjing to Beijing 138

On the 7th, the investigation team departed from Pudong, scheduled to arrive in Beiping on the afternoon of the 9th. There were welcomes in both Bengbu and Xuzhou. According to the planned schedule, the investigation team left Hankou at 9:30 PM on the 5th. He Chengjun and others boarded the "Longhe" ship to see them off. Lord Lytton replied in Chinese, "Wishing you good health." When the investigation team returned from visiting the refugee reception center and Wuhan University in Wuchang, the city was already illuminated with countless lights. Only students from various schools and Boy Scouts were seen standing on the dock. As the wind and sand were severe at that time, the investigation team felt uneasy and boarded the ship first to bid farewell, and then went ashore for dinner. Lord Lytton was the last to return.

The impression the investigation team gained in Wuhan was better than expected, particularly praising the magnificent architecture of Wuhan University. As for the levee works, they thought they were too rudimentary and feared they would be insufficient to prevent flooding. At 9:00 AM on the 6th, when passing Jiujiang, representatives from various circles, including the garrison commander Guo Su, and the county magistrate Jiang Yi, boarded the ship to welcome them. However, representative Gu had already telegraphed Xiong Shihui to decline the honor. Lord Lytton and others freely disembarked to sightsee, but returned after only an hour. Many Westerners bought porcelain as souvenirs.

The representative of the Pingpu Railway under the Ministry of Railways finalized the special train schedule on board, as follows: ㈠ Depart from Pukou at 4:00 PM on the 7th, arrive in Jinan at 4:00 PM on the 8th; ㈡ Depart from Jinan at 7:00 PM on the 8th, arrive in Tianjin at 9:00 AM on the 9th; ㈢ Depart from Tianjin at 2:30 PM on the 9th, arrive in Beiping at 6:00 PM on the 9th.

The reception organization finalized the disembarkation and boarding procedures. It was estimated that the "Longhe" would arrive in Nanjing at 1:00 PM on the 7th. The ship would dock in the middle of the river, and lunch would be on board. After lunch, they would take the "Chengping" ferry to Pukou. When disembarking from the ferry, the investigation team would go first, followed by the Chinese and Japanese representatives. The rest would wait until the luggage was transported before boarding the train with the Pingpu Railway reception staff. When boarding the train, the badge issued by the railway should be pinned on the lapel, and the assigned berth should be found according to the special pass. As for the luggage, it would be transported by the China Travel Service. Items with red paper would be placed in each person's room, while items with green paper would only be available for collection after arriving in Beiping. The badge was round and made of silk, with jujube-red color at the top and bottom. The top said "Welcome" and the bottom said "League of Nations Investigation Team". The center was white and printed with the Pingpu Railway emblem, which was quite beautiful. Personnel who could not be accommodated on the special train would take a special express train, departing at 7:00 PM on the same day. Because it did not stop en route, it would arrive in Beiping before the investigation team (sent from Nanjing on the 7th).

The League of Nations Investigation Team arrived in Nanjing at 12:30 PM on the 7th aboard the "Longhe" ship. The ship docked in the middle of the river. While waiting for the "Chengping" ferry to arrive and unloading the luggage, Lord Lytton and four others, accompanied by Representative Gu Weijun, went to Foreign Minister Luo Wengan's private residence to bid farewell and review all important documents. They then crossed the river and boarded the special train, departing for the north at 4:10 PM.

The train belonged to the Beining Railway and was specially prepared for tourist groups. It was no less luxurious than those in Europe and America. Lord Lytton and Earl McCordie shared a car, General Claudel, Major General McCoy, and Dr. Heaney shared a car, Representative Gu Weijun and his confidential secretary shared a car, Secretary-General Dr. Haas and Deputy Secretary-General Pelt shared a car, and Japanese representative Isaburo Yoshida and his confidential secretary shared a car. In addition to the bedrooms, these five cars all had reception rooms. There was also a conference car, a dining car, several ordinary first-class sleeping cars, and a luggage car. Later, due to the increased number of people, the previous plan to take the Tianjin-Pukou through train was canceled. One first-class blue steel car and three third-class cars were added. The interior was extremely luxurious. Most of the equipment used was domestically made. The attendants were also trained and well-versed in Western customs. The Ministry of Railways also sent Yang Xianfen, Peng Like, the Tianjin-Pukou Railway sent Qian Zongyuan, Yang Jinbo, Yang Tianyun, Zhao Guodong, and the Beining Railway sent Hu Guanglu, Tan Yaozong, and Huang Juechen to take care of them along the way. In addition to the defense army providing protection along the way, the Capital Garrison Command also sent military police to protect the train, and the reception was very thorough.

When the train passed through Chuzhou, Mingguang, and other small stations, flags were raised to show respect. At 10:20 PM, it arrived in Bengbu. Local business representatives Sun Yuanfu, academic representative Ma Jingchang, agricultural representative Li Lingxiao, industrial representative Shao Ziying, press representative Dai Jiufeng, and party representative Xia Shi boarded the train to welcome them and presented welcome speeches.

The investigation team heard that Xuzhou had prepared a grand welcome, but as it was late at night, it was very inconvenient. Representative Gu specially telegraphed Commander Wang Jun to thank all circles and asked them not to trouble themselves (sent from Xuzhou on the 8th).

Ninety-Nine Steel Knives 139

—Zhang Yanxiang

I remember during the 1911 Revolution, Liu Bowen's "Shaobing Song" and the "Tui Bei Tu" were widely circulated. I especially liked the two lines: "Holding ninety-nine steel knives, killing all the barbarian children until they stop." They were quite encouraging. Yesterday, I recalled them again and pondered their meaning. I suddenly remembered that the Shenyang Incident was launched at 11:00 PM on September 18th, known as the "September 18th Incident." But by that time, it had already entered the midnight hour of the 19th, which exactly matches the number "ninety-nine." When the Shanghai Incident occurred, the 19th Route Army killed the invaders for the country with overwhelming force. The names of the three generals implicitly contained the succession of "ninety-nine." The head of General Commander Jiang's name "Jiang" has two "tens," the head of Army Commander Cai's name "Cai" also has two "tens," and the head of Commander Dai's name "Dai" has one "ten." The "Tian" character in the middle is another "ten." The lower "Gong" character has another two "tens." Commander Dai's given name "Ji" has a "ten" at the bottom. The "ten" at the top lacks a stroke, which can be said to be ten minus one, which is nine. The total happens to match "ninety-nine." Is this accidental? General Commander Jiang's given name "Nai" means nine tripods. Army Commander Cai's given name "Ting" means nine courts, which also implicitly shows the number ninety-nine.

The word "Hu" in the second line "barbarian children" can be divided into the two characters "Gu" (ancient) and "Yue" (moon), which can be matched with "Jinri" (today), which is present-day Japan. The right side of Army Commander Cai's name "Kai" is "Bi Ri" (compared to the sun). Commander Dai's name "Ji" contains "Ge Ri" (dagger-axe sun). They all contain the character "Ri" (sun), which is related to the "barbarian children" as Japan. The steel knives are our broadsword teams, which engage in close combat with the Japanese army.

Post-War Notes 140

—Parrot

When the Shanghai War was tense, American soldiers filled the area around Avenue Road and Kaifeng Road with barbed wire, blocking people's doors. Now the Shanghai War has turned to the west. The sound of gunfire has gradually receded and finally cannot be heard. However, the barbed wire in areas such as Avenue Road still blocks people's doors and has not been dismantled. Residents have to take detours or squeeze through the gaps, which is certainly inconvenient. But a middle-aged woman surnamed Gao said, "It's good that this damned barbed wire isn't dismantled. It's not bad to use it to dry my youngest son's diapers."

X X X X

The mother of Little Lion goes out every morning carrying an empty basket. By evening, she always brings home a full basket of burnt wood. Mother Wang next door is envious. She asked Little Lion's mother, "Where do you go to get so much firewood?" Little Lion's mother said proudly, "I also spend capital. I have to buy three bananas and a box of cigarettes for the Japanese soldiers every day."

X X X X

After the Shanghai War, there were several times more dogs than people in Zhabei. When I went to Zhabei, I noticed that the dogs' fur was shiny and very fat. The dogs' eyes were red. When they saw strangers, they would pounce on them like tigers, very fiercely.

Biology says that dogs are a subspecies of wolves. Although they are domesticated by people, they still retain the nature of wolves. Indeed, indeed.

—Ping

The National Crisis Conference, which is difficult to produce, has repeatedly postponed its meeting, and members have been appointed in batches. The current government is eager to try. What achievements has the current government made in its efforts over the years that can be gratifying to the people? It should also reflect deeply on itself. Shanghai War and Military Equipment (3)

—Yi Zang

Pistols

There are many types of pistols. They were originally created in Italy. They are generally used for defense when approaching the enemy and are a convenient and effective tool for self-defense. The military uses signal pistols, gas pistols, and new automatic pistols that can be as effective as light machine guns. The most common and representative pistol used by various countries is the Velgman automatic pistol. The caliber of its muzzle is 7.6 mm. The firing rate is 480 rounds per minute. The range is about 800 meters. This type of pistol can be imitated by factories in Northeast China. After the September 18th Incident, the Beidaying Arsenal was occupied by the Japanese army. It is said that tens of thousands of them were lost. So they used Chinese goods to fight the Chinese. We have to thank Zhang Xueliang for this gift. As for our country's original pistols, they were very simple iron products, like rifles. They used gunpowder and iron bullets. The technology was extremely immature, and their use was not very effective. The copper cap mechanism (made of phosphorus paper and covered with a copper cap) would often not fire if it was damp. And because too much gunpowder was loaded, the iron barrel would often explode. During the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895, two or three of them were seized by the Japanese army. They are now displayed in the Yushukan at Kudanzaka in Tokyo. The reporter still remembers them vividly. As for the pistols captured by our army in the Zhabei and Jiangwan positions during this Shanghai Incident, most of them were Japanese Nambu-style automatic pistols and Type 14 automatic pistols. These pistols were improved by the Japanese based on the six-shot pistols sent by the Indian Viceroy to Toyotomi Hideyoshi and Beloly, referring to the Velgman model.

Record of Twin Buildings Amidst Military Affairs (29) 142

—Master of Seeking Happiness

Chapter 4: Marriage Proposals Press, Causing Hesitation and Self-Disturbance; Enemy Troops Seize Territory, Rekindling Old Conflicts

Who knew that An Yutian, being entangled by her for too long, had no intention of accepting her kindness and was instead annoyed by this trivial matter. He coldly replied, "Let it be. It's getting late. I'm going to sleep soon. I'll change it myself when I get up tomorrow." This kind of rejection, similar to issuing an eviction order, was no different from splashing a ladle of ice water on her boiling heart, greatly disappointing her. However, a lover who is not yet married must maintain a bit of politeness. Moreover, a woman must be even more self-respecting on the surface of etiquette. She could not express any contention at that moment, nor could she linger any longer. Unconsciously, she listened carefully, and there was silence in the courtyard. The neighbors in the public house were probably already asleep. Looking at the clock on the desk again, the hands were almost at one o'clock. With a melancholy and extremely unnatural bitter smile, she said, "I didn't realize I had been groping around until so late. Not only should you rest early, but I should also leave. Fortunately, our affairs have been discussed with some progress. Tomorrow, you just need to ask Mr. Wei to be the matchmaker, and it won't be difficult to settle. I'll still come here to see you in the evening. Everything can be discussed again." An Yutian no longer tried to keep her. He personally escorted her to the gate and hired a car for her. Before leaving, she repeatedly urged him to wait for her in the public house tomorrow night. He answered with a series of "yes" and sent her away. Returning to his room, he hurriedly went to bed to spread out the quilt and sleep. But it always seemed as if something, like a large stone, was lying across his chest, preventing him from falling asleep peacefully. He naturally pondered that this was the matter of Li Wenxia forcing him to announce their engagement. But the engagement was voluntary and had already been secretly agreed to verbally. In his heart, he really had no intention of regretting or shirking it. But strangely, in some inexplicable way, he always seemed to be unwilling to announce it and was unwilling to settle it so quickly. But what exactly was he waiting for? As soon as he closed his eyes, the noble and beautiful Liang Xiaoyun's figure would appear in his mind. However, Liang Xiaoyun was unequal in status. He didn't not know this. He really shouldn't have any expectations of her. It's just that in the darkness, it always seemed as if a god or demon was urging him. He was always unwilling to give up and must temporarily wait. Even though he knew it was useless, he always thought that there would be a wonderful opportunity in the future, and he could get unexpected gains.

Gold Standard Trend Steady and Healthy 143

Continued rise of four taels. Yesterday, the trend of the gold standard was outstanding, once breaking out of 710 taels. Initially, the rise was due to the relentless decline in overseas silver markets, already seeing a new high price of 712.8 taels. Subsequently, the ups and downs were probably due to the different trends in foreign exchange rates for British pounds and US dollars. Because of the sharp drop in exchange rates, the market then turned weak due to large accounts selling off due to the poor situation. At noon, it was only counted between 705 taels. The aftermarket softened further, but the market situation was peaceful, with a high-low range of only about nine taels throughout the day. In the end, it continued to rise by 4 taels. Military Expenses and the Buddha 158

Only the Nineteenth Route Army once had a day to "Raise soldiers for a thousand days to use them for one day." This is an ancient saying with experience and reason. But since we talk about raising soldiers, it is natural that there can be no expenses. Therefore, military expenses were originally a large part of the country's legitimate expenditure, and also a kind of burden that the people should bear.

Yesterday I saw a telegram from Beijing saying that the national military expenditure, after being reviewed and approved by the government, is 10 million yuan per month, to be allocated by the Ministry of Finance. Roughly looking at this telegram, it is not a strange thing. But when I calculate it, 10 million yuan per month is 120 million yuan per year. I don't know how much the government's total annual income is. However, I remember that the government also has so-called education expenses, industrial expenses, etc., which are also very important. I don't know how much the government approves each month. If they also distribute 10 million yuan per month like military expenses, I wonder if the government has such a corresponding income.

I will not worry about this problem for the time being. What I want to talk about now is that the 10 million yuan approved by the government and allocated by the Ministry of Finance, I don't know where the Ministry of Finance will get this 10 million yuan from? I think it must be accumulated from the sweat and blood of our ordinary people, and a part of it is taken out from the hard work of ordinary people to provide it.

Let me ask again, why do ordinary people go to provide such huge expenses? Why do ordinary people willingly take it out to provide it? Because the responsibility of the soldiers was originally the four big characters of "Defend the Country and Protect the People", which is what I said above, "Use it in one day". Alas!

I think of this one day. I am watching this one day.

Mourning Mozi's Idle Talk Supplemented and Corrected by Chen Zhuzun 159

Zhuzun wrote "Mozi's Idle Talk, Supplemented and Corrected", spending more than ten years, searching the words of hundreds of scholars, and compiling a book of hundreds of thousands of words. Mr. Chen Shiyi of Houguan praised him as a friend who could argue with Sun Zhongrong, and Mr. Tang Weizhi of Xishan called him the culmination of Mozi's learning. Five years ago, it was handed over to the Commercial Press for typesetting and printing, and was printed in over a thousand pages in small type. It was about to be bound when the Commercial Press was destroyed by the Japanese army, and my book also suffered the disaster. I wrote a poem to mourn it.

Who pities the anti-war theory repeated thousands of times? Again I see an unprecedented war disaster unfold. Universal love has the same intention as God. (It is said that Mozi's theory has something in common with Christianity) Without blackening, there is no way to quell the ashes of Qin. Years of experience have dimmed the wind and dust. The enmity between Yan and Ying becomes the sorrow of drums and horns. I have failed my friends' kindness for ten years. Letters urging the book's publication have come frequently in vain. (In the past ten years, the study of Mozi has flourished greatly, and many scholars at home and abroad have written to ask about the publication of my book.)

Popular Science

Cadaver Poison Storage 161

The day after the sound of artillery ceased in Zhabei and Wusong, I went to Zhabei to take a look, which made me heartbroken. In the usually bustling streets and alleys, there were Chinese corpses everywhere. The day before yesterday, I went around for another week. These corpses were naturally gone, but in the nearby fields, there were shallow graves everywhere. Walking past them, the air was very different from other places. I therefore thought that these honest Chinese people had already been brutally killed by the enemy's guns and cannons, but they were very unwilling to leave behind the cadaver poison, which was being released with the gradually warmer weather. So I wrote this "Cadaver Poison", partly to express grief for the dead, and partly as a reference for those fighting against Japan.

When animals or human bodies decay, the organic substances contained in them are transformed by a kind of bacteria to form various cadaver poisons. This is a class of alkaline toxins, whose toxicity varies in strength. According to research by Koelker, cadaver poison occurs 24 to 28 hours after the body decays, with the strongest toxicity. The toxin contained is called neurine. After 5 to 6 days, the toxicity is weaker. Although the chemical structure of cadaver poison has not been determined, it produces a significant reaction when using the plant alkali test. Therefore, forensic chemists must use the plant alkali method to conduct various tests when examining corpse toxins, and then determine which plant alkali the deceased died from before his death.

The physiological reactions of cadaver poison on living organisms are often different from those of plant alkaloids. Therefore, many people die from poisoning, because the main toxin contained in cadaver poison, neurine, is very strong. Its toxic physiological action is to paralyze the nervous system and worsen the heart. The symptoms include dizziness, vomiting, diarrhea, dilated pupils, weak pulse, cold limbs, and finally general paralysis, loss of consciousness and death. As for the method of detoxification of cadaver poison, atropine is usually used, because atropine can have the opposite effect to neurine.

Casual Talk

The Extravagant Affairs of the Rich by Lu Pin 162

The rich people in society who seek fame through waste are nominally different from fools, but in reality they are almost the same, because the extravagant things done by the rich and the foolish things done by the fools are actually not much different. Now let's take two examples of extravagant things done by the rich to prove my point of view.

The wife of a certain chairman lives in the Western District of the Shanghai International Settlement, which is close to the small vegetable market. However, she does not go to the nearby small tea market to buy vegetables every morning, saying that the prices are too expensive. Therefore, she takes her car to Mongol Road in Zhabei every day to buy fish and meat. This kind of extravagant method of thrift, if the gasoline used by the car is compared with the money saved from the small vegetable market, can be used as evidence that extravagance and foolishness are similar.

My friend teaches in the home of a certain wealthy man. Recently, this master's family property was sealed due to litigation, and my friend has to go to that humble temporary residence to teach every day. This Dongweng gentleman, in order to save a dinner, sends the teacher home by car (because my friend lives in the west of Shanghai) after completing the reading lesson at 6 pm every day. This is another extravagant calculation, which is similar to that of a fool.

East, West, North, and South

Radio is a Tool of National Subjugation by Mian Yi 163

Many people will find this topic very strange. Radio is the latest crystallization of modern material civilization and scientific development. Thanks to the invention of radio, people have been given a lot of convenience. Every country relies on it as a weapon for military and transportation. How can it be a tool of national subjugation? Moreover, radio is more developed in the UK and the US than in China. Why don't they perish, but instead become richer and stronger, and when they come to China, they become a tool of national subjugation?

No matter what happens, it cannot escape the good and bad sides. For example, the modern new inventions of science, on the good side, it is true that the more developed science is, the more civilized materials are, and people get a lot of enjoyment, but from the bad side, the more developed science is, the easier it is to kill people, and the more barbarous human beings become, which is exactly the opposite. Radio is also the same. If you use it well, you will become richer and stronger. If you don't use it well, it is a tool of national subjugation.

In European and American countries, almost every family is equipped with a radio. Their purpose is to make national news unimpeded, so once a major event occurs, it is broadcast by the radio station, and the people of the whole country know it in an instant. The second is to invite celebrities to give lectures to increase people's knowledge. Entertainment is the least important purpose, but China is exactly the opposite. Entertainment is the most important purpose, and what is broadcast every day is completely entertainment programs. As for celebrity speeches or national events, it is really hard to come by. In the event of January 28, Japan knew about it throughout the country within an hour, but China had to open the newspaper tomorrow to find out. Isn't this an obvious fact?

Because China's purpose of installing radio is entertainment, a group of bourgeois people and idle classes used to have to go out to get the pleasure of seeing and hearing, but now they only need to install a radio, and they don't even have to go out the door, and they can get all kinds of entertainment, so they accompany their wives and concubines at home all day long, indulging in licentious pleasures, and ignoring any major events. It is true that with one machine in hand, all thoughts are empty. Fortunately, China still cannot afford to have everyone equipped with a radio, otherwise, wouldn't the country's major affairs be unattended to? If it doesn't perish at this time, when else will it?

I earnestly hope that the domestic radio industry will pay attention to this point.

Tan Ying

University Students' Love Sickness by Yi Zang 164

Dr. Albert Hegar, the president of Missouri State University in the United States, has published interesting opinions on solving the love sickness of general university students.

He said that to make students concentrate on their studies, the first thing to solve is their love sickness. To solve this problem, is to support their lovers to get married, because most male and female students often flirt with each other in the classroom, and they turn a blind eye and a deaf ear to the teacher's explanation. When the teacher asks a question, they stare blankly and don't know how to answer. When they leave the class, they rush to the lounge to look for the students they love, and offer their affection. If they can't find that lover, most of them skip class and go out.

Every morning, they rush to school to wait outside the door. After school, if there are male and female couples who love each other, they will naturally go out happily in pairs. If there are people who are not matched, they will look like stray dogs, pacing around with their heads down and dejected, making all kinds of homework put aside. Therefore, students who usually have good grades, once infected with this love sickness, none of them can pass the test every time. So, to make students learn, the first thing is to solve their symptoms. This is what I (Dr. Hegar) have gained from past experience. In my opinion, for students in the university who have one-sided thinking patients, it is best to set up a marriage opinion box. Which student looks at which person, can vote by name as much as possible. After opening the votes, if there are three or four male students who want to win the favor of the princess, the student can be allowed to choose freely. This is very fair. Dr. Hegar also said that when the number of university students getting married increases in the future, the school should set up nurseries to avoid them having too many worries.

Market News 165

Medical and Pharmaceutical Review Agency: According to the Medical and Pharmaceutical Review Agency, the Medical and Pharmaceutical Review Agency was initiated in the winter of the Republic of China in 1928 by dozens of medical and pharmaceutical experts in Shanghai, including Dr. Chu Minyi, Wang Qizhang, Yu Yunxiu, Xie Yingrui, and Zhou Mengbai. Soon, Dr. Chu Minyi was publicly elected as the editor-in-chief to publish the Medical and Pharmaceutical Review Semi-Monthly. In the past three years, more than 70 issues have been published. The opinions in it, regardless of new or old medicine and pharmaceuticals, are all ingenious and precise. One paper is popular, and there are thousands of subscribers at home and abroad. Recently, the Japanese have been showing their tyranny and disregarding public reason. The dark curtain of their medical and pharmaceutical names invading our country has been revealed one by one, and a list of Chinese medicines and other countries' medicines that can replace Japanese medicines has been compiled. In addition, texts on scientific defense such as green gas bombs and poison gas have also been researched and published. Subscriptions for the whole year of 24 issues only cost one yuan for postage. To request a sample issue, send a letter to No. 408, Rue Albert, with five cents for postage, and it will be sent immediately.

China English Day and Night School: China English Day and Night School, located at the intersection of Nanshi Road on Nanjing Road, has been established in Shanghai and Hangzhou for many years. It was founded by Dr. Raimon from the West and Dr. Song Ziqiang. The individual classes and special classes specially set up by the school have excellent grades, because its teaching method is suitable for the students' level, very detailed and earnest. The courses and time can be determined by the students themselves, so that the students do not interfere with their legitimate work, and can come and go casually day and night, and be taught as soon as they arrive. Therefore, those who register for the class are very enthusiastic.
